2/The breakfast was very average, with few choices, and the taste of the freshly cooked rice noodles was also average
3/The service level of the hotel was really too poor, from the front desk, to the floor cleaning, to the restaurant, there was no initiative, and they would not take the initiative to greet the guests...

In short, in Leshan, the room price of nearly 700 in the off-season, I can only say - it is really too average, and it is not recommended for guests who have high service requirements!

You can walk along Binjiang Road to the Winter Swimming Square, where you can see the Leshan Giant Buddha from a distance and watch the confluence of three rivers. At night, you can watch the night view of the Leshan Giant Buddha here, and then go to Shangzhongshun Street to eat delicious food. If you have time, you can also go to the Confucian Temple.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:City-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in June 2021
info:Couples
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted June 17, 2021
msg:The treasure hotel in Leshan's Emei Mountain trip is the best in the group. Originally booked a city view room, Wu Xuan at the front desk was very good, and helped to upgrade the river view room to have a chance to experience the scenery of the Minjiang River. The hotel has a good location, right on the bank of the Minjiang River, with a distant view of the Leshan Giant Buddha, and you can fall asleep listening to the river at night. As a very historical hotel, the owner has renovated, all facilities are updated, the bed is very comfortable, the river view room is equipped with a bathtub, you can enjoy the river view while taking a bath. It can also be done on tatami mats, watching the river view and listening to the sound of the water, sipping tea in peace. The wall of the room is azure in Morandi color, the color is elegant, the entrance, the desk, and the tatami wall are all paintings and calligraphy works of the Jiazhou school. The ink landscape on the bedside, the whole house is in an elegant modern new Chinese style, and the owner's aesthetic is online. The bathroom accessories in the room are from the Lâ€™Occitane verbena series, and the towels are thick and soft, and are properly equipped with five stars. In the public facilities of the hotel, the lobby is tall and majestic, with huge Chinese paintings of the Leshan Giant Buddha. On the left side of the lobby are the Jiazhou Hotel Museum and the Jiazhou Painting School Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition, which embodies the fragrance of Leshan's writing, ink and painting everywhere. Breakfast is served in the panoramic restaurant on the top floor of the hotel, which is rich in categories and tastes good, with invincible river view.
Disadvantages: The shower and bathtub in the room are not separated, the design of the bathroom drain is defective, the drainage after the shower is not smooth, the water accumulation is serious, the bathroom floor is not anti-slip trea**ent, the water is very slippery after the accumulation, there is a greater safety hazard, and the elderly with children Need to be extra careful. I hope that the hotel will solve the bathroom drainage problem as soon as possible, eliminate safety hazards, and ensure the safety of guests.
